## GT Analysis

The GT is:
```
0.201*(-1 + P/5.637)*(1 - P/10.233)*P + 0.201*P + 0.201*P/(1 + exp(-5.637*(-0.634 + P)))
```

Let me expand the first term:
- (-1 + P/5.637)(1 - P/10.233) = -1 + P/10.233 + P/5.637 - P²/(5.637×10.233)
- Multiplied by P: -P + P²/10.233 + P²/5.637 - P³/(5.637×10.233)

So GT = 0.201*[-P³/(57.684) + P²(1/10.233 + 1/5.637) - P] + 0.201*P + 0.201*P/(1 + exp(-5.637(-0.634 + P)))

The 0.201*(-P) + 0.201*P cancels out!

GT = 0.201*[-P³/57.684 + P²(1/10.233 + 1/5.637)] + 0.201*P/(1 + exp(-5.637*(-0.634 + P)))

So GT = c₀*P³ + c₁*P² + c₂*P/(1 + exp(c₃*(P - c₄)))

where c₀, c₁ are specific constants, and the last term is a **sigmoid in P** (not t).

Key structural features:
1. **P³ term** (cubic polynomial in P)
2. **P² term**
3. **P × sigmoid(P)** term — this is `P/(1 + exp(-5.637*(P - 0.634)))`
4. **No dependence on t**

Since there's no t-dependence, any candidate with t-dependent terms that can't be zeroed out needs those terms set to 0.

The sigmoid term `P/(1+exp(c*P + d))` is the critical distinguishing feature.

Now let me check each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** P³c₀ + P³c₁ + P²c₂ + P²c₃ + P²c₄ + Pc₅ + Pc₆ + c₇t·exp(c₈t)
Set c₇=0 to kill t-term. Becomes: aP³ + bP² + cP. Missing sigmoid term. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 2:** P³c₀ + P²c₁ + P²c₂ + Pc₃ + Pc₄·exp(Pc₅)
= aP³ + bP² + cP + c₄P·exp(c₅P). The term P·exp(c₅P) is NOT equivalent to P/(1+exp(αP+β)). exp(P) ≠ 1/(1+exp(-P)). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 3:** Has exp(c₅t) — set c₄=0. Becomes aP³+bP²+cP. Missing sigmoid. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 4:** Set c₆=0. Becomes aP³+bP²+cP. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 5:** Has t-dependent terms and log(Pc₉+1). Even setting t-terms to 0: aP³+bP²+cP+0. Missing sigmoid. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 6:** t-dependent. Set t-terms to 0: aP³+bP²+cP. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 7:** Set c₄=0: aP³+bP²+cP. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 8:** Set c₆=0: aP³+bP²+cP. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 9:** Has 1/P⁵ term and t-terms. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 10:** aP³+bP²+cP. Pure polynomial. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 11:** Set c₈=0: aP³+bP²+cP. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 12-15, 16-50:** Let me focus on candidates that have sigmoid-like terms in P.

**Candidate 28:** P³c₀+P²(c₁+c₂)+Pc₃ + c₄t·exp(c₅t) + c₆/(c₇exp(Pc₈+c₉)+1)
Set c₄=0. This gives: aP³+bP²+cP + c₆/(1+c₇exp(c₈P+c₉)). But GT has **P**/(1+exp(...)), not a constant/(1+exp(...)). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 46:** P³c₀+P²c₁+P²c₂+P²c₃/(P+c₄)+Pc₅. This is aP³+bP²+P²c₃/(P+c₄)+cP. The rational term P²/(P+c₄) is not sigmoid. **NO MATCH**
